     439                 :            : /*
     440                 :            :  * Shared control information that is used by senders, receivers and background thread.
     441                 :            :  */
     442                 :            : static ICGlobalControlInfo ic_control_info;
     443                 :            : 
     444                 :            : /*
     445                 :            :  * Macro for unack queue ring, round trip time (RTT) and expiration period (RTO)
     446                 :            :  *
     447                 :            :  * UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM - the number of slots in the unack queue ring.
     448                 :            :  *                              this value should be greater than or equal to 2.
     449                 :            :  * TIMER_SPAN                 - timer period in us
     450                 :            :  * TIMER_CHECKING_PERIOD      - timer checking period in us
     451                 :            :  * UNACK_QUEUE_RING_LENGTH    - the whole time span of the unack queue ring
     452                 :            :  * DEFAULT_RTT                - default rtt in us.
     453                 :            :  * MIN_RTT                    - min rtt in us
     454                 :            :  * MAX_RTT                    - max rtt in us
     455                 :            :  * RTT_SHIFT_COEFFICIENT      - coefficient for RTT computation
     456                 :            :  *
     457                 :            :  * DEFAULT_DEV                - default round trip standard deviation
     458                 :            :  * MAX_DEV                    - max dev
     459                 :            :  * DEV_SHIFT_COEFFICIENT      - coefficient for DEV computation
     460                 :            :  *
     461                 :            :  * MAX_EXPIRATION_PERIOD      - max expiration period in us
     462                 :            :  * MIN_EXPIRATION_PERIOD      - min expiration period in us
     463                 :            :  * MAX_TIME_NO_TIMER_CHECKING - max time without checking timer
     464                 :            :  * DEADLOCK_CHECKING_TIME     - deadlock checking time
     465                 :            :  *
     466                 :            :  * MAX_SEQS_IN_DISORDER_ACK   - max number of sequences that can be transmitted in a
     467                 :            :  *                              disordered packet ack.
     468                 :            :  *
     469                 :            :  *
     470                 :            :  * Considerations on the settings of the values:
     471                 :            :  *
     472                 :            :  * TIMER_SPAN and UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM define the ring period.
     473                 :            :  * Currently, it is UNACK_QUEUE_RING_LENGTH (default 10 seconds).
     474                 :            :  *
     475                 :            :  * The definition of UNACK_QUEUE_RING_LENGTH is quite related to the size of
     476                 :            :  * sender side buffer and the size we may resend in a burst for an expiration event
     477                 :            :  * (which may overwhelm switch or OS if it is too large).
     478                 :            :  * Thus, we do not want to send too much data in a single expiration event. Here, a
     479                 :            :  * relatively large UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM value is used to avoid that.
     480                 :            :  *
     481                 :            :  * If the sender side buffer is X (MB), then on each slot,
     482                 :            :  * there are about X/UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM. Even we have a very large sender buffer,
     483                 :            :  * for example, 100MB, there is about 96M/2000 = 50K per slot.
     484                 :            :  * This is fine for the OS (with buffer 2M for each socket generally) and switch.
     485                 :            :  *
     486                 :            :  * Note that even when the buffers are not evenly distributed in the ring and there are some packet
     487                 :            :  * losses, the congestion control mechanism, the disorder and duplicate packet handling logic will
     488                 :            :  * assure the number of outstanding buffers (in unack queues) to be not very large.
     489                 :            :  *
     490                 :            :  * MIN_RTT/MAX_RTT/DEFAULT_RTT/MIN_EXPIRATION_PERIOD/MAX_EXPIRATION_PERIOD gives some heuristic values about
     491                 :            :  * the computation of RTT and expiration period. RTT and expiration period (RTO) are not
     492                 :            :  * constant for various kinds of hardware and workloads. Thus, they are computed dynamically.
     493                 :            :  * But we also want to bound the values of RTT and MAX_EXPIRATION_PERIOD. It is
     494                 :            :  * because there are some faults that may make RTT a very abnormal value. Thus, RTT and
     495                 :            :  * expiration period are upper and lower bounded.
     496                 :            :  *
     497                 :            :  * MAX_SEQS_IN_DISORDER_ACK should be smaller than (MIN_PACKET_SIZE - sizeof(icpkthdr))/sizeof(uint32).
     498                 :            :  * It is due to the limitation of the ack receive buffer size.
     499                 :            :  *
     500                 :            :  */
     501                 :            : #define UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM (2000)
     502                 :            : #define TIMER_SPAN (Gp_interconnect_timer_period * 1000) /* default: 5ms */
     503                 :            : #define TIMER_CHECKING_PERIOD (Gp_interconnect_timer_checking_period) /* default: 20ms */
     504                 :            : #define UNACK_QUEUE_RING_LENGTH (UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM * TIMER_SPAN)
     505                 :            : 
     506                 :            : #define DEFAULT_RTT (Gp_interconnect_default_rtt * 1000) /* default: 20ms */
     507                 :            : #define MIN_RTT (100) /* 0.1ms */
     508                 :            : #define MAX_RTT (200 * 1000) /* 200ms */
     509                 :            : #define RTT_SHIFT_COEFFICIENT (3) /* RTT_COEFFICIENT 1/8 (0.125) */

     523                 :            : 
     524                 :            : /*
     525                 :            :  * UnackQueueRing
     526                 :            :  *
     527                 :            :  * An unacked queue ring is used to decide which packet is expired in constant time.
     528                 :            :  *
     529                 :            :  * Each slot of the ring represents a fixed time span, for example 1ms, and
     530                 :            :  * each slot has a associated buffer list/queue which contains the packets
     531                 :            :  * which will expire in the time span.
     532                 :            :  *
     533                 :            :  * If the current time pointer (time t) points to slot 1,
     534                 :            :  * then slot 2 represents the time span from t + 1ms to t + 2ms.
     535                 :            :  * When we check whether there are some packets expired, we start from the last
     536                 :            :  * current time recorded, and resend all the packets in the queue
     537                 :            :  * until we reach the slot that the updated current time points to.
     538                 :            :  *
     539                 :            :  */
     540                 :            : typedef struct UnackQueueRing UnackQueueRing;
     541                 :            : struct UnackQueueRing
     542                 :            : {
     543                 :            :         /* save the current time when we check the time wheel for expiration */
     544                 :            :         uint64 currentTime;
     545                 :            : 
     546                 :            :         /* the slot index corresponding to current time */
     547                 :            :         int     idx;
     548                 :            : 
     549                 :            :         /* the number of outstanding packets in unack queue ring */
     550                 :            :         int numOutStanding;
     551                 :            : 
     552                 :            :         /* the number of outstanding packets that use the
     553                 :            :          * shared bandwidth in the congestion window. */
     554                 :            :         int numSharedOutStanding;
     555                 :            : 
     556                 :            :         /* time slots */
     557                 :            :         ICBufferList slots[UNACK_QUEUE_RING_SLOTS_NUM];
     558                 :            : };
     559                 :            : 
     560                 :            : /*
     561                 :            :  * All connections in a process share this unack queue ring instance.
     562                 :            :  */
     563                 :            : static UnackQueueRing unack_queue_ring = {0, 0, 0};
     564                 :            : 
     565                 :            : static int ICSenderSocket = -1;
     566                 :            : static uint16 ICSenderPort = 0;
     567                 :            : static int ICSenderFamily = 0;

     590                 :            :  *

     592                 :            :  * recvQueueSizeCountingTime - counting times when computing totalRecvQueueSize.
     593                 :            :  * totalCapacity             - the capacity sum when packets are tried to be sent.
     594                 :            :  * capacityCountingTime      - counting times used to compute totalCapacity.
     595                 :            :  * totalBuffers              - total buffers available when sending packets.
     596                 :            :  * bufferCountingTime        - counting times when compute totalBuffers.
     597                 :            :  * activeConnectionsNum      - the number of active connections.

     599                 :            :  * mismatchNum               - the number of mismatched packets received.
     600                 :            :  * crcErrors                 - the number of crc errors.

     602                 :            :  * recvPktNum                - the number of packets received by receiver.

     604                 :            :  * duplicatedPktNum          - duplicate packet number.

    2483                 :            :  * RTT is dynamically computed, and expiration period is based on RTT values.
    2484                 :            :  * We cannot simply use RTT as the expiration value, since real workload does
    2485                 :            :  * not always have a stable RTT. A small constant value is multiplied to the RTT value
    2486                 :            :  * to make the resending logic insensitive to the frequent small changes of RTT.
    2487                 :            :  *
    2488                 :            :  */

    2493                 :            :          * In fault injection mode, we often use DEFAULT_RTT,
    2494                 :            :          * because the intentional large percent of packet/ack losses will make

    2496                 :            :          * In real hardware environment/workload, we do not expect such a packet loss pattern.
    2497                 :            :          */

    2500                 :            :         {

    2507 [ -  + ][ +  + ]:     833580 :                 return Max(MIN_EXPIRATION_PERIOD, Min(MAX_EXPIRATION_PERIOD, (conn->rtt + (conn->dev << 2)) << (factor)));

    4025                 :            : 
    4026                 :            : /*
    4027                 :            :  * handleAckedPacket
    4028                 :            :  *              Called by sender to process acked packet.
    4029                 :            :  *
    4030                 :            :  *      Remove it from unack queue and unack queue ring, change the rtt ...
    4031                 :            :  *
    4032                 :            :  *      RTT (Round Trip Time) is computed as the time between we send the packet
    4033                 :            :  *      and receive the acknowledgement for the packet. When an acknowledgement 
    4034                 :            :  *      is received, an estimated RTT value (called SRTT, smoothed RTT) is updated
    4035                 :            :  *      by using the following equation. And we also set a limitation of the max
    4036                 :            :  *      value and min value for SRTT.
    4037                 :            :  *          (1) SRTT = (1 - g) SRTT + g x RTT (0 < g < 1)
    4038                 :            :  *      where RTT is the measured round trip time of the packet. In implementation,
    4039                 :            :  *      g is set to 1/8. In order to compute expiration period, we also compute an
    4040                 :            :  *      estimated delay variance SDEV by using:
    4041                 :            :  *          (2) SDEV = (1 - h) x SDEV + h x |SERR| (0 < h < 1, In implementation, h is set to 1/4)
    4042                 :            :  *      where SERR is calculated by using:
    4043                 :            :  *          (3) SERR = RTT - SRTT
    4044                 :            :  *      Expiration period determines the timing we resend a packet. A long RTT means
    4045                 :            :  *      a long expiration period. Delay variance is used to incorporate the variance
    4046                 :            :  *      of workload/network variances at different time. When a packet is retransmitted,
    4047                 :            :  *      we back off exponentially the expiration period.
    4048                 :            :  *          (4) exp_period = (SRTT + y x SDEV) << retry
    4049                 :            :  *      Here y is a constant (In implementation, we use 4) and retry is the times the
    4050                 :            :  *      packet is retransmitted.
    4051                 :            :  */
    4052                 :            : static void
    4053                 :            : handleAckedPacket(MotionConn *ackConn, ICBuffer *buf, uint64 now)
    4054                 :            : {
    4055                 :     832259 :         uint64 ackTime = 0;

    4569                 :            : /*
    4570                 :            :  * sendBuffers
    4571                 :            :  *              Called by sender to send the buffers in the send queue.
    4572                 :            :  *
    4573                 :            :  * Send the buffers in the send queue of the connection if there is capacity left
    4574                 :            :  * and the congestion control condition is satisfied.
    4575                 :            :  *
    4576                 :            :  * Here, we make sure that a connection can have at least one outstanding buffer.
    4577                 :            :  * This is very important for two reasons:
    4578                 :            :  *
    4579                 :            :  * 1) The handling logic of the ack of the outstanding buffer can always send a buffer
    4580                 :            :  *    in the send queue. Otherwise, there may be a deadlock.
    4581                 :            :  * 2) This makes sure that any connection can have a minimum bandwidth for data
    4582                 :            :  *    sending.
    4583                 :            :  *
    4584                 :            :  * After sending a buffer, the buffer will be placed into both the unack queue and
    4585                 :            :  * the corresponding queue in the unack queue ring.
    4586                 :            :  */

    4646                 :            : /*
    4647                 :            :  * handleDisorderPacket
    4648                 :            :  *              Called by rx thread to assemble and send a disorder message.
    4649                 :            :  *
    4650                 :            :  * In current implementation, we limit the number of lost packet sequence numbers
    4651                 :            :  * in the disorder message by the MIN_PACKET_SIZE. There are two reasons here:
    4652                 :            :  *
    4653                 :            :  * 1) The maximal number of lost packet sequence numbers are actually bounded by the
    4654                 :            :  *    receive queue depth whose maximal value is very large. Since we share the packet
    4655                 :            :  *    receive and ack receive in the background thread, the size of disorder should be
    4656                 :            :  *    also limited by the max packet size.
    4657                 :            :  * 2) We can use Gp_max_packet_size here to limit the number of lost packet sequence numbers.
    4658                 :            :  *    But considering we do not want to let senders send many packets when getting a lost
    4659                 :            :  *    message. Here we use MIN_PACKET_SIZE.

    4661                 :            :  *
    4662                 :            :  * the format of a disorder message:
    4663                 :            :  * I) pkt header

    4665                 :            :  *  - extraSeq -> the largest seq of the received packets

    4976                 :            : /*
    4977                 :            :  * checkDeadlock
    4978                 :            :  *              Check whether deadlock occurs on a connection.
    4979                 :            :  *
    4980                 :            :  * What this function does is to send a status query message to rx thread when the connection has
    4981                 :            :  * not received any acks for some time. This is to avoid potential deadlock when there are continuous
    4982                 :            :  * ack losses. Packet resending logic does not help avoiding deadlock here since the packets in the unack
    4983                 :            :  * queue may already been removed when the sender knows that they have been already buffered in the
    4984                 :            :  * receiver side queue.
    4985                 :            :  *
    4986                 :            :  * Some considerations on deadlock check time period:
    4987                 :            :  *
    4988                 :            :  * Potential deadlock occurs rarely. According to our experiments on various workloads
    4989                 :            :  * and hardware. It occurred only when fault injection is enabled and a large number packets and
    4990                 :            :  * acknowledgments are discarded. Thus, here we use a relatively large deadlock check period.
    4991                 :            :  *
    4992                 :            :  */
